A.3 REQUIRED SUPPLIES OR SERVICES
The District of Columbia Courts, on behalf of the Office of the General Counsel, seeks
a qualified vendor to provide a cloud-hosted, configurable commercial-off-the-shelf
("COTS") Legal Case and Document Management System, including necessary
software, licenses, warranties, and related services to include installation, document
migration, implementation, on-site post-implementation support and training, and
maintenance and support as specified in Section C (Description/Specifications/Work
Statement).
PLEASE NOTE: A COURT CASE MANAGEMENT SYSTEM IS NOT WITHIN
THE SCOPE OF THIS PROCUREMENT OR ANY RESULTING CONTRACT.
A.4 OPEN MARKET
This solicitation is issued on an unrestricted/open market basis.
A.5
CONTRACT AWARD
The Courts anticipates the award of a single firm-fixed price contract for a base year
and 4 option years to the responsible offeror whose offer conforms to the solicitation
and will be most advantageous to the Courts, considering price and other evaluation
factors. See Sections L and M. The Courts anticipate making an immediate award as
deemed required.
A.6 SAM REGISTRATION
In order to receive a contract award, the prospective contractor/offeror must be
registered through the Federal System For Award Management (SAM) at
https://www.sam.gov. SAM.gov is an official U.S. government website. There is no
cost to use SAM. You can use SAM.gov for FREE to:
Register to do business with the U.S. government.
Update or renew your entity registration.
Check status of an entity registration.
Search for entity registration and exclusion records.
A.7 COMMUNICATIONS AND QUESTIONS FROM OFFERORS
All written communications regarding this solicitation should be submitted by email to
Ms. Grace Alao, Senior Contract Specialist, at grace.alao@dccsystem.gov. See Section
L.4.
Questions from prospective contractors/offerors must be submitted no later than
11:00 a.m. EST on April 13, 2026. The Courts will not consider any questions
received after that time.

The Courts will post all amendments, addenda, and responses to offeror questions on
the D.C. Courts website https://www.dccourts.gov/dc-courts/solicitations. Oral
explanations or instructions given by Courts officials or staff before the award of the
contract will not be binding.

(b) The Contractor must provide cloud-managed services, e.g., migration,
configuration, optimization, security, and maintenance of their application hosted in
a government cloud service provider.
(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

under this Contract. Complete records of all services performed by the Contractor
must be maintained and made available to the Courts during contract performance
and for as long afterwards as the Contract requires.
(c) The Courts have the right to review and test all services called for by the contract to
the extent practicable during the term of the Contract. The Courts may perform

E.1
Inspection of Services
(a) "Services" as used in this clause includes all services provided under this Contract,
including, but not limited to, project management, installation, implementation,
document migration, on-site post-implementation support, on-site user training,
maintenance, end user support, and all other work performed under Section C
(Description/Specifications/Work Statement).
(b) The Contractor must provide and maintain documentation of all services provided
under this Contract. Complete records of all services performed by the Contractor
must be maintained and made available to the Courts during contract performance
and for as long afterwards as the Contract requires.
(c) The Courts have the right to review and test all services called for by the contract to
the extent practicable during the term of the Contract. The Courts may perform
reviews and system and integration tests in a manner that will not unduly delay the
work.
(d) If any services do not conform to the contract requirements, the Courts may require
the Contractor to perform these services again in conformity with contract
requirements, at no increase in contract amount. When the defects in services cannot
be corrected by performance, the Courts may require the Contractor to take necessary
action to ensure that future performance conforms to contract requirements and
reduce the contract price to reflect value of services performed.
(e) If the Contractor fails to promptly perform the services again or take the necessary
action to ensure future performance in conformity to contract requirements, the
Courts may (1) by contract or otherwise, perform the services and charge the
Contractor any cost incurred by the Courts that is directly related to the performance
of such services, or (2) terminate the Contract for default.
END OF SECTION E
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60, Legal Case & Document Management System

SECTION F - DELIVERABLES AND PERFORMANCE
F.1
Contract Period of Performance
The term of the Contract is twelve (12) months from date of award of the contract.
F.2
Option to Extend the Term of the Contract
The Courts may extend the term of this Contract for up to four (4) optional one-year
periods, or a fraction or multiple fractions thereof, at the sole discretion of the Courts and
subject to the availability of appropriated funds. If the Courts exercise an option, the
extended contract will be considered to include this option provision. The exercise of any
option under this contract is contingent on the appropriation of funds for the respective
option period. However, the availability of funds does not obligate the Courts to exercise
this option year.

Additional Licenses

price offered for that year.

SECTION G - CONTRACT ADMINISTRATION DATA
G.1
Payment/Invoices
(a) The Courts will make invoice payments under the terms and conditions specified in the
contract. The Contractor will be compensated upon completion and acceptance of the
work as specified in the contract. Payments shall be considered as being made on the
day a check is dated or the date of an electronic funds transfer. The Contractor shall be
compensated as set forth below.
(b) All invoices and payment request must be submitted electronically through the U.S.
Department of the Treasury's Invoice Processing Platform (IPP) System using the
"Bill to Agency" of Interior Business Center-FMD. The IPP website address is
https://www.ipp.gov. In addition, it is the vendors' (contractors') responsibility to be
System for Awards Management (SAM) registered and in IPP. The vendors
(contractors) must be SAM registered in order to register in IPP. The SAM website
address is https://www.sam.gov.
(c) After contract and purchase order award, in order to receive payment, the Contractor
must use the IPP website to register, access, and use IPP for submitting all invoice
requests for payment(s). Assistance with enrollment can be obtained by contacting the
IPP Production Helpdesk via email at IPPCustomerSupport@fiscal.treasury.gov or by
phone (866) 973-3131.
(d) Payment request means any request for contract financing payment or invoice payment
by the Contractor. To constitute a proper invoice, at a minimum, the Contractors'
electronic invoice shall include the following information:
(i)
Name and address of the Contractor;
(ii) Purchase Order number;
(iii) Invoice date;
(iv) Invoice number;
(v) Name of the Contracting Officer Technical Representative (COTR);
(vi) COTR's email address; and
(vii) Description, quality, unit of measure, and extended price of the services
or supplies actually rendered.
(e) Once the electronic invoice has been submitted through IPP, no later than 2 business
days from the electronic submission, the Contractor must email and/or mail to the
COTR a copy of the electronic invoice along with all the required supporting
documentation as stated in the contract.
(f) The COTR shall review each electronic invoice for certification of receipt of satisfactory
services prior to authorization of payment.
reviews and system and integration tests in a manner that will not unduly delay the

(b) The Contractor must provide cloud-managed services, e.g., migration,
configuration, optimization, security, and maintenance of their application hosted in
a government cloud service provider.
(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C

and for as long afterwards as the Contract requires.

the extent practicable during the term of the Contract. The Courts may perform

C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C

C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.

SECTION C - DESCRIPTION / SPECIFICATIONS / WORK STATEMENT
C.1
Scope of Work
The Contractor must provide a cloud-hosted, configurable commercial-off-the-shelf
("COTS") Legal Case and Document Management System, including necessary
software, licenses, and warranties ("System") to the District of Columbia Courts ("D.C.
Courts" or "Courts"). The Contractor must also provide related services, to include
installation, document migration, implementation, on-site post-implementation support
and on-site end user training. In addition, the Contractor must provide ongoing high
quality maintenance and end user support.
PLEASE NOTE: A COURT CASE MANAGEMENT SYSTEM IS NOT WITHIN
THE SCOPE OF THIS CONTRACT.
C.2
Overview of District of Columbia Court System (DCCS)
The D.C. Courts is the judicial branch of the District of Columbia and comprises three
entities: the District of Columbia Court of Appeals, the Superior Court of the District of
Columbia, and the District of Columbia Court System ("DCCS"). DCCS includes the
Executive Office and administrative offices that support both courts. The D.C. Courts is
a fully unified large urban court system with over 95 judicial officers and
approximately 1,200 employees. As Washington, D.C. is a city that also functions as a
state, the D.C. Courts provide city and state-level services. The Courts also receive
funding directly from the Federal government.
DCCS provides business support services, including but not limited to capital projects,
budget and finance, procurement and contracts, administrative services, human
resources, training, planning, research and development, court reporting, information
technology, and legal counsel through the Office of the General Counsel.
C.3
The Office of the General Counsel (OGC)
OGC provides a broad spectrum of legal advisory services to the D.C. Courts such as
legislative drafting and analysis; contract, lease, inter-agency agreements, and grant
reviews; interpretation and drafting of orders, policies, and agreements; and supporting
records management, data release, and compliance protocols. OGC manages and
supports the rulemaking process, drafting proposed and final amendments, public
notices, memoranda, correspondence, and promulgation orders. OGC advises
management on employment, grievance, and disciplinary matters. OGC represents the
Courts before administrative tribunals and disciplinary hearings and serves as in-house
counsel in litigation and other matters in which the Courts have an institutional interest,
including managing eDiscovery. OGC attorneys serve as legal advisors to Courts'
leadership and management, and Boards of Judges. OGC attorneys also serve on
Courts' ad hoc and standing committees. The General Counsel serves as the D.C.
Courts' Ethics Officer and chairs the Courts' Legal Advisory Council.
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 6 of 46
OGC is currently comprised of six (6) staff members: the General Counsel, three
Associate General Counsels, a Paralegal Specialist, and an Administrative Assistant.
All six staff members require software licenses, access to the System, user training, and
user support. The Courts may require up to 10 (ten) software licenses in future option
years.
OGC source documents and files include approximately 1.2 TB of confidential,
privileged, and litigation sensitive materials comprised of approximately 390,000 files
saved across 10,000 folders on an NTFS network drive. There is no legacy legal or
document management system. The vast majority are PDF and MS Word files but other
file types may include Excel, MP4, and VTT. These include approximately 22,000
PDF files of recently digitized paper files, which are in OCR format and generally
indexed by topic and titles of the former paper folders. Document scanning is not
required under this Contract.
C.4
Objectives
OGC seeks to modernize its operations and gain business and legal process efficiencies.
OGC's objectives are that the System achieve the following:
(a) Provide electronic law practice management functionality to support operational
needs, including contract and eDiscovery management.
(b) Satisfy core document and case management requirements with minimal
customization.
(c) Automate workflows and business processes using information
technology and artificial intelligence (AI) to the maximum extent
possible.
(d) Utilize AI unstructured document extraction and automation.
(e) Promote document version control with highly secure, accurate, and
reliable recordkeeping.
(f) Enhance case tracking.
(g) Data analytics and reporting capabilities.
(h) File migration.
(i) Migrate and organize files and documents and reduce redundancy.
(j) Interface with widely used office applications to promote efficiency.
(k) Promote intuitive, user friendly, and accessible technology with easy user
navigation and a modern look and quality.
C.5
System Requirements and User Needs

Type

Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C

C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.

SECTION E - INSPECTION AND ACCEPTANCE
E.1
Inspection of Services
(a) "Services" as used in this clause includes all services provided under this Contract,
including, but not limited to, project management, installation, implementation,
document migration, on-site post-implementation support, on-site user training,
maintenance, end user support, and all other work performed under Section C
(Description/Specifications/Work Statement).
(b) The Contractor must provide and maintain documentation of all services provided
under this Contract. Complete records of all services performed by the Contractor
must be maintained and made available to the Courts during contract performance
and for as long afterwards as the Contract requires.
(c) The Courts have the right to review and test all services called for by the contract to
the extent practicable during the term of the Contract. The Courts may perform
Windows 2012, 2016, 2019, 2022 and higher Standard and
Operating Systems
Data Center Edition
Client -Windows 11
End User Platforms
Dell Workstations, peripherals

MS Windows 11

newer)

Environment

2022 (and newer), Azure SQL Managed Instances, MyQL
Data Warehousing
and Business

Intelligence

Security

Load balancer
Citrix NetScaler VPX version 11 (and newer)
Mobile devices
Dell, Apple, and other laptops/tablets; Apple and Android
phones, Apple iPad
MS Office
M365
(b) The Contractor must provide cloud-managed services, e.g., migration,
configuration, optimization, security, and maintenance of their application hosted in
a government cloud service provider.
(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

(b) The Contractor must provide cloud-managed services, e.g., migration,
configuration, optimization, security, and maintenance of their application hosted in
a government cloud service provider.
(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C

C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.

under this Contract. Complete records of all services performed by the Contractor
must be maintained and made available to the Courts during contract performance
and for as long afterwards as the Contract requires.
(c) The Courts have the right to review and test all services called for by the contract to
the extent practicable during the term of the Contract. The Courts may perform

hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at

components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

(b) The Contractor must provide cloud-managed services, e.g., migration,
configuration, optimization, security, and maintenance of their application hosted in
a government cloud service provider.
(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C

C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.

C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C

(b) The Contractor must provide cloud-managed services, e.g., migration,
configuration, optimization, security, and maintenance of their application hosted in
a government cloud service provider.
(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

(c) The Contractor is responsible for supporting the infrastructure to run the application
hosted in their cloud service provider's government cloud. This must include, at
minimum, regular maintenance, security patching, updating infrastructure
components necessary to run the application, and conducting performance
monitoring and system health checks.
C.7
Required Services
(a) Project Management. The Contractor must assign a Project Manager
responsible for the successful delivery, installation, and implementation of
the System and post-implementation support and training. The Project
Manager must maintain regular communication and contact with the
Contracting Officer's Technical Representative ("COTR") throughout the
entire process, including post-implementation support and training. The
Project Manager and all contractor resources must understand OGC's
objectives (see Section C.4) and be experienced in installing and
implementing legal case and document management systems.
(b) Kickoff Meeting. The Contractor must conduct a project initiation/kick-off
meeting with the COTR and OGC staff to understand OGC's objectives and
expectations for the System and to outline the steps and deliverables.
(d) Installation and Implementation. The Contractor must install and implement the
system and cooperate fully with the Courts' Information Technology ("IT")
Division throughout the System installation and implementation process. The IT
Division is responsible for all aspects of business process automation, information
systems management, network operations, security auditing, as well as desktop and
peripheral support.
(e) Document Migration. The Contractor must migrate existing files into the new
System, including but not limited to:
(i) document coding, including identification of specific information of
the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System

the source documents and creating a data/document code profile.
(ii) identification and deletion of duplicates files.
(iii) development of an overall strategy for electronic records management
Solicitation No.: DCSC-26-RFP-60 Legal Case & Document Management System
Page 11 of 46
including but not limited to policies, procedures, and taxonomy
(uniform naming conventions).
(f) On-site post-Implementation Support and Training. The Contractor must
provide five (5) consecutive days of on-site, post-implementation support
and in-person, facilitated end user training on the System, including how to
migrate, import, and maintain documents on the System. A virtual training
must be provided for future new users. The Contractor must provide
administrator training as requested.
(g) Maintenance and End User Support. The Contractor must provide a Service
Level Agreement (SLA) to include high quality maintenance and end user
support following system implementation and throughout the duration of the
contract term. This must include, at minimum:
(i) Built-in system help functions.
(ii) Searchable knowledge base.
(iii) Telephone numbers, email contact information, and online chat
features.
(iv) Tier 1 and Tier 2 end user support, including for all in-scope
requirements, capabilities, modules, functionality, and services. This
shall include a phone-based help desk Mondays through Saturdays
from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM Eastern Time.
(v) Written documentation on releases, system updates, enhancements,
software patches, and corrections to software bugs.
(vi) Full cooperation with the Courts' IT Division.
END OF SECTION C
